&amp; \quad &amp;\textrm{Covectors are members of dual vector space \((V^*, S, +, \cdot)\)} \\ &amp;\quad V \enspace \textrm{set of vectors}                                      &amp;  &amp;\quad V^* \enspace \textrm{set of covectors (functions) - } V \to \mathbb{R} \\ &amp;\quad S \enspace \textrm{set of scalars}                                      &amp;  &amp;\quad S \enspace \textrm{set of scalars} \\ &amp;\quad + \enspace (\boldsymbol{v} + \boldsymbol{w})^{\mu} = v^{\mu} + w^{\mu}  &amp;  &amp;\quad + \enspace (a + b)(\boldsymbol{v}) = a(\boldsymbol{v}) + b(\boldsymbol{v}) \\ &amp;\quad \cdot \enspace  (n \boldsymbol{v})^{\mu} = n v^{\mu}                    &amp;  &amp;\quad \cdot \enspace (n a) (\boldsymbol{v}) = n a(\boldsymbol{v}) \\[1.5ex] &amp;                                                                              &amp; \quad &amp;\textrm{Additional properties (linearity):} \\ &amp;                                                                              &amp;  &amp;\quad a(\boldsymbol{v} + \boldsymbol{w}) = a(\boldsymbol{v}) + a(\boldsymbol{w}) \\ &amp;                                                                              &amp;  &amp;\quad a(n \boldsymbol{v}) = n a(\boldsymbol{v}) \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut"
